[30;1m91 | [0m[35m[0m

[30;1m70 | [0m[35mVersioneer works by adding a special `_version.py` file into your source[0m
[30;1m71 | [0m[35mtree, where your `__init__.py` can import it. This `_version.py` knows how to[0m
[30;1m72 | [0m[35mdynamically ask the VCS tool for version information at import time.[0m
[30;1m73 | [0m[35m[0m
[30;1m74 | [0m[35m`_version.py` also contains `$Revision$` markers, and the installation[0m
[30;1m75 | [0m[35mprocess marks `_version.py` to have this marker rewritten with a tag name[0m
